## Callbacks

These functions are called by the engine automatically:

| Callback | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `luna.load()` | Called once after the script is loaded |
| `luna.update(dt)` | Called every frame; `dt` is elapsed seconds |
| `luna.draw()` | Called every frame for rendering |
| `luna.keypressed(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is pressed |
| `luna.keyreleased(key)` | Called when a keyboard key is released |
| `luna.mousepressed(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is pressed |
| `luna.mousereleased(x, y, button)` | Called when a mouse button is released |
| `luna.touchpressed(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch start |
| `luna.touchmoved(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch move |
| `luna.touchreleased(id, x, y, dx, dy, pressure)` | Called on touch end |
| `luna.resize(w, h)` | Called when window is resized |
| `luna.focus(focused)` | Called when window gains/loses focus |
| `luna.quit()` | Called when the window is closed |
| `luna.gamepadpressed(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button press |
| `luna.gamepadreleased(id, button)` | Called on gamepad button release |
| `luna.gamepadaxis(id, axis, value)` | Called on gamepad axis change |

## luna.graphics_ext

Lua API bindings for Phase 24 graphics extension types.

Provides UserData wrappers and factory functions for extended graphics
subsystems: Light2D, TextureAtlas, DrawLayer, Viewport, ViewportScale,
SpriteSheet, PolygonMap, GraphRenderer, LargeMapRenderer, ColumnBatch,
Camera2D, Animation, Trail, DecalSurface, and PaletteLUT.

*157 entries | 157 documented*

## luna.window

Window Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for window api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*34 entries | 34 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.window.close()`

Requests the application to close the window.

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L386)*

---

#### `luna.window.fromPixels(value)`

@param value : number @return any

**Parameters:** `value`

*Source: [src/lua_api/window_api.rs](src/lua_api/window_api.rs#L300)*

#### `luna.window.getDisplayCount()`

## luna.math_ext

Extended math API bindings — Phase 25 types and utility functions.

Adds 7 factory functions and 23 module-level functions to `luna.math`.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for math ext api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*102 entries | 102 documented*

## luna.audio

Audio Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for audio api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaSource`, `LuaBus`, `LuaMidiPlayer`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*124 entries | 124 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.audio.clearFilter(id_val)`

Removes any active filter from the audio source.

@param id_val : any

**Parameters:** `id_val`

*Source: [src/lua_api/audio_api.rs](src/lua_api/audio_api.rs#L1607)*

#### `luna.audio.getMasterVolume()`

Returns the current master volume scale (0.0 - 1.0) applied to all audio output.

## luna.thread

Registers the `luna.thread` namespace.

Provides Lua-level multithreading: create background threads that run
independent Lua VMs and communicate via thread-safe channels.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for thread api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaThreadHandle`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*7 entries | 7 documented*

---

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L127)*

---

The thread gets its own Lua VM and can communicate via channels. @param code : string @return any

**Parameters:** `code`

*Source: [src/lua_api/thread_api.rs](src/lua_api/thread_api.rs#L114)*

### AIWorld Methods

#### `AIWorld:addAgent(name)`

Registers a new agent named `name` in this world and returns its handle.

@param name : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `name` — `string`: Unique identifier for the new agent.

**Returns:** An `Agent` handle ready for further configuration.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L204)*

---

#### `AIWorld:getAgent(name)`

Looks up a registered agent by name.

@param name : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `name` — `string`: Name of the agent to retrieve.

**Returns:** The `Agent` handle, or `nil` if no agent with that name exists.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L222)*

---

#### `AIWorld:getAgentCount()`

Returns the number of agents currently registered in this world.

@return any

**Returns:** `integer` — total agent count.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L251)*

---

#### `AIWorld:getGlobalBlackboard()`

Returns a snapshot of the shared world-level blackboard.

@return any

**Returns:** A `Blackboard` containing data visible to all agents in this world.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L260)*

---

#### `AIWorld:removeAgent(agent)`

Removes and destroys the given agent from this world.

@param agent : Agent

**Parameters:**

- `agent` — `Agent`: Handle of the agent to remove, obtained from `addAgent`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L239)*

---

#### `AIWorld:update(dt)`

Advances all agents in the world by `dt` seconds, integrating velocity into position.

@param dt : number

**Parameters:**

- `dt` — `number`: Elapsed seconds since the last frame.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L272)*

---

---

#### `Agent:setPosition(x, y)`

Teleports the agent to world-space coordinates (`x`, `y`).

@param x : number @param y : number

**Parameters:**

- `x` — `number`: Horizontal world-space position.
- `y` — `number`: Vertical world-space position.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L301)*

---

#### `Agent:setPriority(p)`

Sets the scheduling priority; higher-priority agents are processed first during `update`.

@param p : integer

**Parameters:**

- `p` — `integer`: Priority value, higher = earlier processing.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L411)*

---

#### `Agent:setVelocity(x, y)`

Sets the agent's velocity vector in world units per second.

@param x : number @param y : number

**Parameters:**

- `x` — `number`: Horizontal component.
- `y` — `number`: Vertical component.

*Source: [src/lua_api/ai_api.rs](src/lua_api/ai_api.rs#L330)*

## luna.data

Registers the `luna.data.*` binary data, compression, hashing, and encoding API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for data api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*8 entries | 8 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.data.compress(format_str, raw_data, [level])`

Compresses data using the given algorithm ('deflate', 'gzip', 'lz4').

@param format_str : string @param raw_data : string @param level : integer? @return any

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `raw_data`, `level`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L55)*

---

#### `luna.data.decode(format_str, encoded)`

Decodes binary data from a buffer according to a pack-format string.

@param format_str : string @param encoded : string

**Parameters:**

- `format` — Pack-format string (same syntax as string.pack).
- `data` — Binary string or ByteData buffer to read from.

**Returns:** Decoded Lua values followed by the next unread byte offset.

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L130)*

---

#### `luna.data.decompress(format_str, compressed_data)`

Decompresses data using the given algorithm.

@param format_str : string @param compressed_data : string @return any

**Parameters:** `format_str`, `compressed_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L74)*

---

#### `luna.data.encode(format_str, raw_data)`

Encodes Lua values into a binary string using a pack-format string.

@param format_str : string @param raw_data : string @return any

**Parameters:**

- `format` — Pack-format string (same syntax as string.pack).
- `...` — Values to encode.

**Returns:** Binary string containing the packed bytes.

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L110)*

---

#### `luna.data.encodeToml(table)`

Encodes a Lua table as a TOML string.

@param table : table

**Parameters:** `table`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L154)*

---

#### `luna.data.hash(algo_str, raw_data)`

Returns the cryptographic hash (md5, sha1, sha256) of the input.

@param algo_str : string @param raw_data : string @return any

**Parameters:** `algo_str`, `raw_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L90)*

---

#### `luna.data.newByteData(value)`

Creates a new mutable byte buffer of the given size.

@param value : any

**Parameters:** `value`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L28)*

---

#### `luna.data.parseToml(input)`

Parses a TOML string and returns a Lua table.

@param input : string

**Parameters:** `input`

*Source: [src/lua_api/data_api.rs](src/lua_api/data_api.rs#L143)*

## luna.sound

Registers the `luna.sound.*` decoded audio sample manipulation API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for sound api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*4 entries | 4 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.sound.clearMidiSoundFont()`

Unloads the active SoundFont so the MIDI player falls back to built-in defaults.

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L146)*

---

#### `luna.sound.hasMidiSoundFont()`

Returns whether a SoundFont is currently loaded for the MIDI synthesizer.

**Returns:** true if a SoundFont is loaded, false otherwise.
@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L135)*

---

#### `luna.sound.newSoundData(args)`

Creates a raw PCM audio buffer for building procedurally generated sound.

**Parameters:**

- `samples` — Total number of PCM samples to allocate.
- `sampleRate` — Sample rate in Hz (e.g. 44100).
- `bitDepth` — Bit depth per sample (8 or 16).
- `channels` — Number of channels (1 = mono, 2 = stereo).

**Returns:** New SoundData object ID.
@param args : MultiValue

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L43)*

---

#### `luna.sound.setMidiSoundFont(path)`

Sets the SoundFont (.sf2) file that the MIDI synthesizer uses for instrument samples.

**Parameters:**

- `path` — File path to the .sf2 SoundFont file.
@param path : string

*Source: [src/lua_api/sound_api.rs](src/lua_api/sound_api.rs#L110)*

---


## luna.graph

Registers the `luna.graph.*` directed-graph and item-flow simulation API.

Exposes `LuaGraph`, `LuaNode`, `LuaEdge`, and `LuaGraphItem` UserData types
wrapping `crate::graph::Graph` with callback dispatch for simulation events.

## luna.battle

Lua bindings for the `luna.battle.*` turn-based battle API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for battle api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaStatusEffect`, `LuaCombatAction`, `LuaCombatant`, `LuaCombatBattle`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*76 entries | 76 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.battle.newAction(name)`

New action.

@param name : string @return any

**Parameters:** `name`

*Source: [src/lua_api/battle_api.rs](src/lua_api/battle_api.rs#L558)*

---

@param name : string? @return any

**Parameters:** `name`

*Source: [src/lua_api/battle_api.rs](src/lua_api/battle_api.rs#L579)*

---

@param name : string @return any

## luna.cardgame

Lua bindings for `luna.cardgame.*`.

Exposes Card, Stack, StackBuilder, StackManager, CardPool, Slot, StackHistory,
and group-analysis utilities to Lua scripts via the `luna.cardgame` namespace.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for cardgame api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaCard`, `LuaStack`, `LuaDeckBuilder`, `LuaZoneManager`, `LuaCardPool`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*212 entries | 212 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.cardgame.clearTypes()`

Clears all registered item types.

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1949)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.defineType(name, def_tbl)`

Defines a card type in the global registry.

@param name : string @param def_tbl : table

```lua luna.cardgame.defineType("fireball", { category = "spell", subtype  = "damage", rarity   = "rare", maxPerDeck = 3, stats    = { damage = 10, manaCost = 3 }, tags     = { "fire", "instant" }, meta     = { artist = "A. Smith" }, }) ```

**Parameters:** `name`, `def_tbl`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L1869)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.findAtLeastNOfStat(items_tbl, stat, n)`

Finds groups where at least `n` items share the same stat integer value.

@param items_tbl : table @param stat : string @param n : integer @return any

**Parameters:** `items_tbl`, `stat`, `n`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L2128)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.findNOfStat(items_tbl, stat, n)`

Finds groups where exactly `n` items share the same stat integer value.

@param items_tbl : table @param stat : string @param n : integer @return any

Returns an array of `{label, score, items}` tables.

**Parameters:** `items_tbl`, `stat`, `n`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L2105)*

---

#### `luna.cardgame.findSequences(items_tbl, stat, min_run)`

Finds consecutive integer stat sequences of length ≥ `min_run`.

@param items_tbl : table @param stat : string @param min_run : integer @return any

Returns an array of `{label, score, items}` tables.

**Parameters:** `items_tbl`, `stat`, `min_run`

*Source: [src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs](src/lua_api/cardgame_api.rs#L2153)*

---

## luna.combat

Lua bindings for the `luna.combat.*` vehicle combat API.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for combat api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaCollisionGroupSet`, `LuaChassis`, `LuaTurret`, `LuaWeapon`, `LuaProjectile`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*110 entries | 110 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.combat.newChassis(body_id, max_hp)`

Creates a new `Chassis` with the given body ID and max HP.

@param body_id : integer @param max_hp : number @return any

**Parameters:**

- `body_id` — `integer`: Physics body ID.
- `max_hp` — `number`: Maximum hit points.

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L682)*

---

#### `luna.combat.newCollisionGroupSet()`

Creates a new `CollisionGroupSet`.

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L670)*

---

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L723)*

---

#### `luna.combat.newProjectilePool(size, [proj_type])`

Creates a new `ProjectilePool` with the given capacity.

@param size : integer @param proj_type : string? @return any

**Parameters:**

- `size` — `integer`: Pool capacity.
- `proj_type` — `string` optional: Projectile type (default `"ballistic"`).

*Source: [src/lua_api/combat_api.rs](src/lua_api/combat_api.rs#L716)*

@param body_id : integer @param joint_id : integer @return any

#### `ProjectilePool:spawn(x, y, angle, speed, damage, damage_type, range)`

Spawns a projectile from the pool. Returns the index or nil if exhausted.

@param x : number @param y : number @param angle : number @param speed : number @param damage : number @param damage_type : string @param range : number @return any

**Parameters:** `x`, `y`, `angle`, `speed`, `damage`, `damage_type`, `range`

## luna.crafting

Lua bindings for `luna.crafting.*`.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for crafting api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaRecipe`, `LuaRecipeRegistry`, `LuaStation`, `LuaCraftSkill`, `LuaCraftQueue`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*177 entries | 177 documented*

### Functions

### ModifierPool Methods

**Parameters:**

- `seed` — `integer`: Deterministic seed value.

**Returns:** `table` — `{name, weight, effects}`, or `nil` if pool is empty.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L1964)*

---

### Recipe Methods

#### `Recipe:addByproduct(item_type, qty, [chance])`

Adds a byproduct output (produced alongside main outputs, not guaranteed).

@param item_type : string @param qty : integer @param chance : number?

**Parameters:**

- `item_type` — `string`: Item ID.
- `qty` — `integer`: Quantity.
- `chance` — `number` optional: Probability 0–1 (default `1.0`).

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L327)*

---

#### `Recipe:addCondition(cond_type, value)`

Adds a crafting condition requirement for this recipe (e.g. biome, weather).

@param cond_type : string @param value : string

**Parameters:**

- `condition_type` — `string`: Condition type identifier.
- `value` — `string`: Required value.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L339)*

---

#### `Recipe:addIngredient(item_type, qty, [consumed])`

Adds an ingredient requirement to this recipe.

@param item_type : string @param qty : integer @param consumed : boolean?

**Parameters:**

- `id` — `string`: Item ID of the ingredient.
- `count` — `integer`: Number of units required.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L227)*

---

#### `Recipe:addOutput(item_type, qty, [quality])`

Adds an output item produced when this recipe is completed.

@param item_type : string @param qty : integer @param quality : string?

**Parameters:**

- `id` — `string`: Item ID of the output.
- `count` — `integer`: Number of units produced.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L242)*

---

#### `Recipe:addTag(tag)`

**Parameters:**

- `tag` — `string`: Tag to add.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L204)*

### RecipeRegistry Methods

#### `RecipeRegistry:add(recipe)`

Registers a recipe in this registry. Raises an error if a recipe with the same ID already exists.

**Parameters:**

- `recipe` — `Recipe`: Recipe object to register.

### Station Methods

#### `Station:addFuel(amount)`

Adds fuel to this station, clamped to capacity.

@param amount : number

**Parameters:**

- `amount` — `number`: Fuel to add.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L829)*

---

#### `Station:canProcess(recipe)`

Returns `true` if this station can currently process the given recipe (level and type match).

@param recipe : Recipe @return any

**Parameters:**

- `recipe` — `Recipe`: Recipe to check against this station's type and level.

**Returns:** `boolean`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L683)*

---

#### `Station:consumeFuel(amount)`

Consumes fuel from this station. Returns `false` if insufficient fuel.

@param amount : number @return any

**Parameters:**

- `amount` — `number`: Fuel to consume.

**Returns:** `boolean` — `true` if consumed successfully.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L842)*

---

#### `Station:effectiveTime(recipe)`

Returns the effective crafting time for `recipe` after applying this station's speed multiplier.

@param recipe : Recipe @return any

**Parameters:**

- `recipe` — `Recipe`: The recipe to evaluate.

**Returns:** `number` — effective time in seconds.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L697)*

---

#### `Station:getFuelCapacity()`

Returns the maximum fuel capacity of this station.

@return any

**Returns:** `number`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs](src/lua_api/crafting_api.rs#L816)*

## luna.debug

Registers the `luna.devtools.*` runtime diagnostics and developer tools API.

Five subsystems: structured logger, hierarchical profiler, frame statistics,
file watcher, and Lua debug bridge. All module-level functions — no
registered types.

*33 entries | 33 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.debug.clearLog()`

## luna.debugbridge

Registers the `luna.debugbridge.*` TCP debug server API.

Embeds a JSON-over-TCP server (127.0.0.1 only) inside the running game.
External tools (VS Code extension, MCP server) connect to inspect and
control the game at runtime. Network I/O runs on a background thread;
Lua-dependent methods are queued and dispatched via `poll()` on the main thread.

*15 entries | 15 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.debugbridge.broadcast(event, json_data)`

Broadcasts a JSON event to all connected clients.

@param event : string @param json_data : string

**Parameters:** `event`, `json_data`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L794)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.capturePrint(msg, [source], [line])`

Captures a print message and broadcasts it to connected clients.

@param msg : string @param source : string? @param line : integer?

**Parameters:** `msg`, `source`, `line`

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L620)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.clearPrintHistory()`

Clears the print history.

*Source: [src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs](src/lua_api/debugbridge_api.rs#L689)*

---

#### `luna.debugbridge.getClientCount()`

@return any

## luna.dialog

Lua API bindings for the `luna.dialog.*` dialog sequencer module.

Provides a `Sequencer` UserData type for visual novel-style text
presentation with typewriter effect, branching choices, timed pauses,
and inline callbacks.

*19 entries | 19 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.dialog.newSequencer()`

## luna.docs

Registers the `luna.docs.*` documentation management API.

Provides engine-integrated documentation management: scanning runtime bindings,
loading TOML doc catalogs, validating completeness, computing quality metrics,
and exporting structured data for VS Code extension IntelliSense.

*67 entries | 67 documented*

## luna.entity

Registers the `luna.entity.*` ECS universe API.

Exposes `Universe` as Lua UserData (`LuaUniverse`) with entity lifecycle,
component operations, querying, systems, tags, layers, and blueprints.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for entity api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*40 entries | 40 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.entity.newUniverse()`

@return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/entity_api.rs](src/lua_api/entity_api.rs#L611)*

## luna.inventory

Lua API bindings for the `luna.inventory.*` slot-based inventory module.

Provides `Item`, `ItemStack`, `Slot`, `Container`, `ItemSet`, and `Inventory`
UserData objects for building RPG-style inventory systems in Lua.

*84 entries | 84 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.inventory.newContainer(name, [mode_str], [slot_count])`

@param name : string @param mode_str : string? @param slot_count : integer? @return any

*Source: [src/lua_api/inventory_api.rs](src/lua_api/inventory_api.rs#L1438)*

## luna.item

Lua bindings for `luna.item.*`.

Exposes Item, Stack, StackBuilder, StackManager, ItemPool, Slot, StackHistory,
and group-analysis utilities to Lua scripts via the `luna.item` namespace.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for item api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaItem`, `LuaStack`, `LuaStackBuilder`, `LuaStackManager`, `LuaItemPool`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*117 entries | 117 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.item.clearTypes()`

Clears all registered item types.

*Source: [src/lua_api/item_api.rs](src/lua_api/item_api.rs#L925)*

---

#### `luna.item.defineType(name, def_tbl)`

Defines an item type in the global registry.

@param name : string @param def_tbl : table

```lua luna.item.defineType("sword", { category = "weapon", stats    = { damage = 10, weight = 5 }, tags     = { "metal", "sharp" }, meta     = { rarity = "common" }, }) ```

**Parameters:** `name`, `def_tbl`

*Source: [src/lua_api/item_api.rs](src/lua_api/item_api.rs#L872)*

---

@param items_tbl : table @param stat : string @param n : integer @return any

## luna.log

Structured game-level logging API (`luna.log.*`).

Exposes convenience logging functions so Lua scripts can emit messages at
specific severity levels and query or change the active log level at
runtime without going through the `luna.system` namespace.

*7 entries | 7 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.log.debug(message)`

Emit a debug-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L31)*

---

#### `luna.log.error(message)`

Emit an error-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L73)*

---

#### `luna.log.getLevel()`

Return the name of the currently active minimum log level.

**Returns:** One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L127)*

---

#### `luna.log.info(message)`

Emit an info-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L45)*

---

#### `luna.log.print(level, message)`

Emit a log message from Lua at the specified severity level.

@param level : string @param message : string

Accepts the same level strings as `luna.log.setLevel`: `"debug"`, `"info"`, `"warn"`, `"error"`, `"trace"`. Unknown levels fall back to `info`.

**Parameters:**

- `level` — Severity level string.
- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L93)*

---

#### `luna.log.setLevel(level)`

Set the minimum severity level for runtime log messages.

@param level : string

**Parameters:**

- `level` — One of `"off"`, `"error"`, `"warn"`, `"info"`, `"debug"`, `"trace"`.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L114)*

---

#### `luna.log.warn(message)`

Emit a warn-severity log message from Lua.

@param message : string

**Parameters:**

- `message` — The message string to log.

*Source: [src/lua_api/log_api.rs](src/lua_api/log_api.rs#L59)*

## luna.minimap

Lua API bindings for the `luna.minimap.*` minimap module.

Provides a `Minimap` UserData type with factory functions for creating
grid-based minimaps with terrain coloring, fog of war, tracked objects,
pings, markers, and viewport rectangle overlay.

*41 entries | 41 documented*

## luna.modding

Modding Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for modding api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*33 entries | 33 documented*

### Functions

@param info : table @return any

**Parameters:** `info`

*Source: [src/lua_api/modding_api.rs](src/lua_api/modding_api.rs#L566)*

### mlua Methods

## luna.pathfinding

Registers the `luna.pathfinding.*` grid-based pathfinding API.

Exposes `NavGrid`, `UnitPathfinder`, and `FlowField` as Lua UserData
with 1-based tile coordinates at the Lua boundary.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for pathfinding api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*34 entries | 34 documented*

### Functions

## luna.patterns

Registers the `luna.patterns.*` software design patterns API.

Provides factory functions and UserData wrappers for reusable patterns:
EventBus (prioritized pub-sub), ObjectPool (object reuse), CommandStack
(undo/redo), ServiceLocator (DI container), Factory (named constructors),
and SimpleState (finite state machine).

*47 entries | 47 documented*

### Functions

## luna.postfx

Lua API bindings for the `luna.postfx.*` post-processing effects module.

Provides `PostFxEffect` and `PostFxStack` UserData types with factory
functions for creating built-in effects, custom shader passes, and
effect stacks that manage ping-pong canvas post-processing pipelines.

## luna.quest

Lua API bindings for `luna.quest.*`.

Exposes quest creation, stage management, objective tracking, and journal
entries through the `luna.quest` table.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for quest api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaObjective`, `LuaQuestStage`, `LuaQuest`, `LuaQuestLog`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*75 entries | 75 documented*

## luna.resource

Lua API bindings for the `luna.resource.*` resource economy module.

Provides `ResourceManager` UserData for managing named resources with
capacity, flow rates, decay, interest, conversions, and overflow policies.

## luna.savegame

Savegame Api implementation for the `lua_api` subsystem.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for savegame api-related operations and data management.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*13 entries | 13 documented*

### Functions

#### `luna.savegame.newSaveManager()`

New save manager.

*Source: [src/lua_api/savegame_api.rs](src/lua_api/savegame_api.rs#L270)*

---

### mlua Methods

#### `mlua:collect()`

Snapshots all registered tables into an in-memory serializable form, ready for disk write.

@return any

**Returns:** `table` — the collected save data.

*Source: [src/lua_api/savegame_api.rs](src/lua_api/savegame_api.rs#L117)*

---

## luna.scene

Registers the `luna.scene.*` scene stack, registry, data store, and depth-sorter API.

The scene stack manages a LIFO stack of Lua scene tables with optional
visual transitions. Scene tables are stored via `mlua::RegistryKey` and
identified by `SceneId`. Inter-scene data is stored similarly.

The `DepthSorter` UserData batches draw callbacks by depth for ordered
compositing each frame.

*28 entries | 28 documented*

### Functions

### DepthSorter Methods

#### `DepthSorter:add(callback, depth)`

Registers a draw callback at the given depth layer. Higher `depth` values draw in front.

@param callback : function @param depth : number

**Parameters:**

- `callback` — `function`: Draw callback `function()` called when flushing this layer.
- `depth` — `number`: Depth value determining draw order (lower = drawn first).

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L66)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:addObject(obj)`

Registers a table object with a `draw` method at the given depth.

@param obj : table

**Parameters:**

- `obj` — `table`: Object with a `draw()` method. Uses `obj.depth` if no explicit depth is provided.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L80)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:clear()`

Removes all registered callbacks and objects without calling them.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L130)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:flush()`

Calls all registered draw callbacks and object `draw()` methods in sorted depth order, then clears the list.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L97)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:getCount()`

Returns the number of callbacks and objects currently registered.

@return any

**Returns:** `integer` — number of registered draw entries.

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L141)*

---

#### `DepthSorter:sort()`

Sorts all registered callbacks and objects by their depth values (ascending).

*Source: [src/lua_api/scene_api.rs](src/lua_api/scene_api.rs#L91)*

---


## luna.stats

Lua API bindings for the `luna.stats` RPG character sheet system.

Exposes [`Sheet`] and a global [`StatsRegistry`] as `luna.stats.*` Lua values.

This module is part of Luna2D's `lua_api` subsystem and provides the implementation
details for stats api-related operations and data management.
Key types exported from this module: `LuaSheet`.
Primary functions: `register()`.

All public items are documented. See the parent module for architectural context
and the `luna.*` Lua API for the scripting interface.

*66 entries | 66 documented*

### Functions
